### [106] [Does Bielik Know What It Doesn't Know? Activation Dispersion Separates Entity Familiarity from Factual Reliability Across Model Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07670)
*Grzegorz Brzezinka*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究大语言模型在生成答案前，其内部激活是否已“知道”实体是否熟悉，以及该信号能否预测事实可靠性。在4个波兰Bielik模型（1.5B-11B）、4个实体域上，无监督的MLP激活离散度指标（逆参与比和谱熵）能以AUROC 0.95-1.00区分已知与虚构实体，但在已知实体内部区分正确与幻觉答案则困难得多（探针0.93，离散度无效）。实体熟悉度与事实可靠性遵循不同的缩放曲线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大模型在生成任何答案token之前，其内部表征是否已“知道”实体是否熟悉，以及这种内部信号能否预测后续答案的事实可靠性，从而理解模型幻觉的根源。

Method: 在4个波兰Bielik模型（1.5B-11B）上，对4个实体域（运动员、城市、作家、音乐家）各使用42个知名、42个模糊但真实、42个虚构实体，每个实体一个单句问题（共504个提示/模型）。使用两种无监督单前向传播的MLP激活离散度指标（逆参与比和谱熵）以及有监督线性探针来分析。

Result: 无监督离散度指标AUROC达0.95-1.00区分已知与虚构实体；有监督探针达0.99-1.00。但已知实体内部区分正确与幻觉答案：探针仅0.93，离散度不优于首token熵基线。5样本语义熵基线仅0.71-0.83，成本高5倍。2520次回答中仅2次拒绝、1次含糊。

Conclusion: 实体熟悉性与事实可靠性是不同现象，遵循不同缩放曲线：熟悉性信号在1.5B已达上限，而事实可靠性随模型规模急剧提升。模型内部知道实体是否熟悉，但几乎从不主动拒绝回答，且难以从内部信号预测具体答案是否正确。

Abstract: Large language models hallucinate most about entities they have never seen. We ask whether a model's activations betray entity familiarity before a single answer token is generated, and whether that signal predicts the factual reliability of the answers. On four Polish Bielik models (1.5B-11B parameters), we probe four entity domains (athletes, cities, writers, musicians), each with 42 well-known, 42 obscure-but-real, and 42 fabricated entities addressed by a one-sentence question (504 prompts per model). Two unsupervised, single-forward-pass dispersion measures over post-SwiGLU MLP activations, inverse participation ratio and spectral entropy, separate known from fabricated entities at AUROC 0.95-1.00 across all domains and scales; a supervised linear probe reaches 0.99-1.00. Both clear selection-aware permutation floors of about 0.70-0.74 (empirical p<=1e-3), survive held-out layer selection (0.93-0.99), and persist on real names (known vs. obscure-but-real: 0.96-1.00). The signal transfers across entity types (mean off-diagonal AUROC 0.92-0.99); a matched-template counterfactual shows the only large drops are template-caused, not entity-type effects, and the signal is diffuse across heads. This representational signal is already at ceiling at 1.5B, whereas behavioral factual reliability scales sharply: 0, 2, 10, and 19 of 42 known athletes are answered fully correctly by the 1.5B, 4.5B, 7B, and 11B models under a strict judge. Within known entities, separating correct from hallucinated answers is much harder (probe 0.93; dispersion no better than a first-token-entropy baseline). A five-sample semantic-entropy baseline reaches only 0.71-0.83 at 5x the inference cost. Despite this internal awareness, the models almost never abstain: an audit of 2,520 answers finds 2 refusals and 1 hedge. Entity familiarity and factual reliability are distinct phenomena on different scaling curves.

### [107] [From Noisy Traces to Root Causes: Structural Trajectory Analysis and Causal Extraction for Agent Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07702)
*Ying Chang,Jiahang Xu,Xuan Feng,Chenyuan Yang,Peng Cheng,Yuqing Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: STRACE是一个通过结构性轨迹分析与因果提取来构建高信噪比优化上下文的框架，能够有效提升长时域智能体的反思式优化效果，在VeruSAGE-Bench任务上将成功率从42.5%提升至58.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的长时域智能体优化依赖反思机制（LLM作为优化器），但真实执行轨迹难以直接使用：批量轨迹冗余异构易导致过拟合，单条轨迹中大量无关步骤干扰优化，而简单截断或滑动窗口会丢弃因果关键信息，产生误导性优化信号。

Method: STRACE框架从两个层面提升信噪比：1) 批量层面：挖掘失败模式，过滤冗余轨迹，保留代表性失败样本；2) 单轨迹层面：在文本依赖图上进行因果定位，移除非因果步骤，识别真正的根因模块用于优化。

Result: STRACE显著优于标准上下文过滤基线。在VeruSAGE-Bench形式化验证任务上，成功优化了人类专家设计的智能体，成功率从42.5%提升到58.5%（提升1.4倍）。

Conclusion: STRACE通过结构化的轨迹分析与因果提取有效解决了长时域智能体优化中的信噪比困境，在复杂任务上展示了对人类专家设计智能体的显著优化能力，代码已开源。

Abstract: The optimization of long-horizon agents increasingly relies on reflection-based mechanisms, where a large language model (LLM) acts as an optimizer to diagnose agent failures and improve agent policies. However, real execution traces are difficult to use directly for optimization: large trace collections are often redundant and heterogeneous, making optimization inefficient and prone to overfitting to low-value failures; meanwhile, each individual trajectory also contains many irrelevant steps, while naive context reduction methods such as truncation or sliding windows can discard causally important evidence and produce misleading optimization signals. To resolve this dilemma, we introduce STRACE (Structural TRajectory Analysis and Causal Extraction), a framework that constructs high signal-noise optimization contexts for more precise and effective optimization. At the batch level, STRACE mines failure patterns to filter redundant traces and retain representative failures; within each selected trace, it performs causal localization over a textual dependency graph to remove non-causal steps and identify the true root-cause module for optimization. Empirical results demonstrate that STRACE significantly outperforms standard context-filtering baselines. Notably, on a challenging formal verification task (VeruSAGE-Bench), it successfully optimizes human-expert designed agents, delivering $1.4\times$ success-rate improvement (42.5% to 58.5%). The code is available at https://github.com/moomight/STRACE .

### [109] [Accurate, Interdisciplinary and Transparent Structure-property Understanding with Deep Native Structural Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07708)
*Chen Tang,Yizhou Wang,Jianyu Wu,Lintao Wang,Shixiang Tang,Pengze Li,Encheng Su,Jun Yao,Jiabei Xiao,Yuqi Shi,Jielan Li,Hongxia Hao,Zhangyang Gao,Fang Wu,Ben Fei,Xiangyu Yue,Pan Tan,Bozitao Zhong,Jinouwen Zhang,Aoran Wang,Yan Lu,Jiaheng Liu,Xinzhu Ma,Liang Hong,Mingyue Zheng,Phil Torr,Bowen Zhou,Wanli Ouyang,Lei Bai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了SciReasoner，一个多模态科学基础模型，能够对蛋白质、小分子和无机晶体进行原生结构推理，通过将坐标、拓扑和周期性连接离散化为统一的结构感知词汇，在86个基准测试中的67个任务上达到最先进性能，并生成可解释的推理轨迹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 结构-性质关系是生物学、化学和材料科学的基础，但现有的AI方法在同时保留领域原生结构信息和展示证据如何支持预测方面面临表征与推理的双重挑战。

Method: SciReasoner将坐标、拓扑和周期性连接离散化为统一的结构感知词汇，将结构标记作为可寻址的证据单元进行推理，实现跨蛋白质、小分子和无机晶体的多模态科学推理。

Result: 在GO注释中将Fmax从0.42提升至0.55；逆合成准确率从0.63提升至0.72；86个基准测试中67个任务达到SOTA；专家评估中98%的推理轨迹优于或可比于前沿大语言模型。

Conclusion: SciReasoner通过将结构变为可检查的推理底物，在科学约束下连接了准确预测与可解释的科学推理。

Abstract: Structure-property relationships are foundational to biology, chemistry and materials science, where function, reactivity and physical response emerge from spatial, chemical and periodic organization. Mechanistically explaining these relationships requires interpreting structural evidence through scientific principles and physical constraints, from stereochemistry and bonding to symmetry, energetics and periodic order. However, applying artificial intelligence to this process presents a joint challenge of representation and reasoning: models must preserve domain-native structural information while showing how specific evidence supports predictions under these constraints. Here we introduce SciReasoner, a multimodal scientific foundation model for native structural reasoning across proteins, small molecules and inorganic crystals. SciReasoner discretizes coordinates, topologies and periodic connectivities into a unified structure-aware vocabulary, treating structural tokens as addressable evidence units during reasoning. In homology-controlled Gene Ontology prediction, SciReasoner improves Cellular Component annotation for low-homology and orphan-like proteins, increasing $F_{\max}$ from 0.42 to 0.55. In chemistry, it raises single-step retrosynthesis accuracy from 0.63 to 0.72 while generating fragment-level disconnection and precursor-verification traces. In materials science, its representations separate elemental and compound phases and resolve high- and low-band-gap regimes. Across 86 benchmarks, SciReasoner achieves state-of-the-art performance on 67 tasks. Double-blind expert evaluation rates its reasoning traces as preferred or at least comparable to those of a frontier large language model in 98% of cases. By making structure an inspectable substrate for reasoning under scientific constraints, SciReasoner connects accurate prediction with interpretable scientific inference.

### [110] [AgentLens: Production-Assessed Trajectory Reviews for Coding Agent Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06624)
*Andrey Podivilov,Vadim Lomshakov,Sergey Savin,Matvei Startsev,Roman Pozharskiy,Maksim Parshin,Sergey Nikolenko*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AgentLens是一个面向交互式代码智能体的生产级基准测试，它超越了传统的二值通过/失败评估，通过形式化验证与LLM轨迹评审相结合的方式，全面评估智能体的整个执行轨迹（指令遵循、工具使用、错误恢复等），并提供可读的评分解释，适用于模型诊断、版本对比和产品回归检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码智能体基准测试将运行简化为单一比特（通过/失败），忽略了用户实际体验到的完整轨迹，包括指令遵循、工具使用、自我验证、错误恢复和交互过程等关键维度。

Method: 将形式化验证（客观检查）与LLM撰写的轨迹评审及侧对比相结合，对每次运行生成可读的评分解释，实现对智能体完整执行轨迹的多维度评估。

Result: AgentLens不仅可用于模型排名，还能用于诊断模型行为、比较同一智能体的连续版本，并在夜间评估流程中捕获产品回归。

Conclusion: AgentLens提供了比传统二值评估更丰富、更可解释的代码智能体评估方案，并已开源。

Abstract: We present AgentLens, a production-assessed benchmark for interactive code agents. Most code-agent benchmarks reduce a run to a single bit -- did the task pass? -- but the people who actually use these agents experience the entire trajectory: how the agent follows instructions, uses its tools, verifies its own work, recovers from mistakes, and talks to them along the way. AgentLens evaluates that whole trajectory. It pairs formal verification, where an objective check exists, with LLM-written trajectory reviews and side-by-side comparisons, so that each run yields a readable explanation of why the score is what it is. This makes AgentLens useful for more than ranking models: we use it to diagnose model behavior, compare successive versions of our own agent, and catch product regressions in a nightly evaluation pipeline. We release the benchmark as open source at https://github.com/agent-lens/agent-lens-bench.

</details>


### [111] [When Does In-Context Search Help? A Sampling-Complexity Theory of Reflection-Driven Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06720)
*Yotam Wolf,Noam Wies,Amnon Shashua*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文从理论上分析了LLM的上下文搜索（in-context search）机制，将其建模为推理轨迹上的近似推断，证明了在早期错误能被可靠定位时，上下文搜索能以多项式次数的顺序尝试实现指数级性能提升，并验证了理论预测在真实大模型上的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为LLM通过自生成、自我批评和修改解决思路的上下文搜索能力提供严格的理论分析，理解其何时有效、为何有效以及其采样复杂度边界。

Method: 将上下文搜索建模为推理轨迹上的近似贝叶斯推断（基模型提供先验，自我反思提供后验更新），理论分析顺序采样复杂度；通过交叉熵训练学习搜索轨迹；将强化学习的最优策略扩展等价于后验重加权规则。

Result: 1）当反思能可靠定位早期错误时，上下文搜索以多项式顺序尝试次数实现指数级提升（解决零样本通过率指数小的难题）；2）当该条件不满足时，条件采样无渐进优势；3）近似后验更新足够，搜索轨迹的交叉熵训练可多项式样本恢复所需行为；4）RL最优策略扩展等价于后验重加权。

Conclusion: 上下文搜索的理论优势取决于错误定位的可靠性，且这些增益具有鲁棒性和可学习性，为理解LLM推理时搜索行为提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Training large language models (LLMs) with extended reasoning has enabled in-context search, in which models iteratively generate, critique, and revise solution attempts. We provide a theoretical analysis of in-context search by modeling it as approximate inference over reasoning traces, where the base model defines a prior and self-reflection provides feedback for posterior updates, and study the resulting inference-time sampling complexity - the number of sequential attempts needed to achieve high success probability. We show that when reflections reliably localize early mistakes, in-context search can yield exponential improvements over the base model, solving problems with exponentially small zero-shot pass rates using only a polynomial number of sequential attempts, whereas when this property fails, conditioning on past attempts offers no asymptotic benefit over parallel sampling. We further show that these gains are robust and learnable: approximate posterior updates suffice, and cross-entropy training on search rollouts recovers the required behavior with polynomial sample complexity. Finally, we show that under a stagewise abstraction of reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, the optimal policy extension implements the same posterior reweighting rule. We validate key qualitative predictions of the theory on real large reasoning models.

### [113] [QANTIS: Hardware-Calibrated Sequential POMDP Belief Updates on IBM Heron](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06760)
*Bayram Yuksel Eker,Suayb S. Arslan,Ozgur Nazli,Mustafa Serhat Demirgil,Furkan Deligoz*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过IBM Heron硬件实验，验证了QANTIS框架在部分可观测Tiger POMDP任务中，使用量子处理器作为信念更新服务时，能够保持后验分布一致性，且在所有决策点上硬件后验与精确贝叶斯后验选择的动作完全一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子处理器作为信念更新服务的复用可行性，验证在部分可观测自主系统中，量子加速的信念更新能否在不破坏下游规划器所需后验一致性的前提下工作。

Method: 在IBM Heron硬件上运行Tiger POMDP，比较三种放大策略（无放大、Guarded Grover放大、全步固定点放大FPAA），通过8/12/20/32步实验检查硬件后验与精确贝叶斯后验在动作选择上的一致性，并使用BIQAE处理边界附近的振幅估计。

Result: 全步FPAA在8步和12步主实验中保持Tiger后验一致，20步和32步控制实验仍在同一工作区间内；所有决策检查中硬件后验与精确贝叶斯后验选择的动作完全一致；BIQAE稳定了零和一附近的振幅估计。

Conclusion: QANTIS能够作为硬件校准的信念更新原语复用，其输出与经典贝叶斯后验在决策层面一致，但本文不宣称硬件优势，而是提供了一个可工作的操作包络。

Abstract: Autonomous systems under partial observability act on beliefs, not raw sensor events. QANTIS treats the quantum processor as a calibrated belief-update service in that loop: it receives a prior and an observation model, estimates the rare-event evidence term, and returns an ordinary posterior to a classical planner. This paper asks whether that service can be reused across a sequential Tiger POMDP horizon on present IBM Heron hardware without corrupting the planner-facing posterior. We answer with a controlled hardware case study rather than an end-to-end autonomy or wall-clock speedup claim. The study compares no amplification, guarded Grover amplification, and all-step fixed-point amplification on the same trajectory, then checks whether the returned posterior would change the downstream action. All-step FPAA preserves the Tiger posterior across the reported 8-step and 12-step primary runs, and the 20-step and 32-step controls remain inside the same operating band. In every reported decision check, the hardware posterior and the exact Bayes posterior select the same immediate action. Boundary-aware BIQAE stabilizes amplitude estimation near zero and near one, while a rare-event sweep maps the logical sample-complexity envelope for one-in-a-million evidence. The result is an operating envelope for a hardware-calibrated belief-update primitive, not a standalone hardware-advantage claim.

### [114] [Cost-Effective Agent Harnesses for Abstract Reasoning and Generalization on ARC-AGI-1](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06764)
*Kabir Moghe,Peter Chin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了第三种范式——不使用思维链模式的DeepSeek V3.2模型，在严格预算下、无ARC特定微调，仅通过架构设计（Explorer-Definer Pipeline和Reflective Orchestrator）将ARC-AGI-1基线从15.50%提升至67.25% pass@2，成本仅每任务0.62美元。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ARC-AGI-1进展依赖两种范式：一是大量测试时计算（前沿模型+进化搜索/穷举采样/长链思维），二是基准专用训练（小模型微调+任务特化架构）。本文探索第三种范式——使用开放权重模型（非思维模式）在严格预算下、无ARC微调，仅通过架构设计来提升性能，验证纯架构改进的可行性。

Method: 1. Explorer-Definer Pipeline：两阶段智能体流水线，分离模式发现（explorer）与可执行变换合成（definer）；2. Reflective Orchestrator：在pipeline基础上增加自主探索新变换的反思机制，当先前假设在训练对上失败时自动探索；3. 使用非思维模式的DeepSeek V3.2，无ARC微调，严格成本控制。

Result: 1. Pipeline：57.50% pass@2，每任务$0.25；2. Orchestrator：67.25% pass@2，每任务$0.62；3. 将15.50%的单次基线提升约52个百分点；4. pass@k分析表明pipeline受限于生成（generation-bound）而非选择（selection-bound），选择捕获约95%候选上限；5. Orchestrator通过自适应重新探索实现生成扩展，pass@1提升9.81个百分点；6. think工具移除导致pass@2下降5.75个百分点。

Conclusion: 纯架构设计可以在无基准专用训练和高测试时计算的情况下显著提升开放权重模型的ARC-AGI-1性能。系统瓶颈在于生成（generation）而非选择（selection），未来改进应聚焦于更广泛的候选变换生成。思考工具（think tool）是pipeline中的关键组件。

Abstract: Recent progress on ARC-AGI-1 from disclosed architectures has come broadly from two regimes: heavy test-time compute over frontier models (evolutionary search, exhaustive sampling, extended chain-of-thought), or benchmark-specific training in which small models are fine-tuned on ARC data, often with task-specialized architectures. We study a third regime: an open-weight model in non-thinking mode (DeepSeek V3.2) under a strict budget, with no ARC-specific fine-tuning. We study what is recoverable through architecture alone, building agentic harnesses that decompose pattern-discovery and program-synthesis stages explicitly. First, we introduce an Explorer-Definer Pipeline that separates pattern discovery from executable transformation synthesis, implemented as a two-stage agent pipeline. Next, we present the Reflective Orchestrator, which augments the pipeline with autonomous exploration of new transformations when previous hypotheses fail on training pairs. On the ARC-AGI-1 public 400-task evaluation set, the pipeline reaches 57.50% pass@2 at \$0.25 per task, and the orchestrator reaches 67.25% pass@2 at \$0.62 per task. Together these architectures lift a 15.50% one-shot baseline by ~52 points without benchmark-specific training or heavy test-time compute. Furthermore, the orchestrator-driven lift tests a falsifiable diagnostic the pipeline produces; unbiased pass@k analysis suggests the pipeline is generation-bound, not selection-bound (selection via training-pair accuracy captures ~95% of the candidate ceiling) and predicts that significant improvement requires broader generation, not better ranking. The orchestrator implements this prediction via adaptive re-exploration and confirms it (unbiased pass@1 lift +9.81 pp, matching selection-mediated pass@2 lift). An additional pipeline ablation identifies its think tool as a significant component, with removal reducing pass@2 by 5.75 pp.

</details>


### [115] [Evaluating SageMath-Augmented LLM Agents for Computational and Experimental Mathematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06820)
*Pavel Snopov,German Magai*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出ReAct风格的智能体框架，将LLM推理与SageMath的可验证反馈结合，并使用Context7获取最新文档。同时改进RealMath基准，引入多步后处理和多阶段验证流程以提升数据质量。

Conclusion: CAS增强的智能体是辅助数学家进行计算探索的有前景方向，本文工作是迈向自动化猜想发现的一步。

Abstract: Recent advances in AI for Mathematics have focused largely on autoformalization and theorem proving, leaving the role of Computer Algebra Systems (CAS) in agentic LLM workflows underexplored. We propose a ReAct-style agentic setup that combines LLM reasoning with verifiable feedback from SageMath, together with Context7 for the up-to-date documentation. We evaluate this agentic setup across frontier models for solving research-level mathematical problems from the RealMath benchmark in a setting that emulates a computational-mathematics research loop. We also propose a refinement to the RealMath benchmark by introducing a multi-step post-processing procedure and a multi-stage validation pipeline, both of which improve the quality and reliability of the extracted problem set. Our experiments reveal substantial performance gains from SageMath access across all evaluated models on +9.7~pp on average, the gains range from 1.5~pp to 27.8~pp and narrow the gap between open-weight and closed models. Qwen~3.7-Max benefits from SageMath the most, while GPT-5.5 achieves the highest solve rate of $75.2\%$ and the lowest token usage among tool-enabled configurations. Our findings suggest that CAS-augmented agents represent a promising direction for assisting mathematicians in computational exploration, and we believe that this work is a step towards automated conjecture discovery. The project repository is available online.

### [116] [The Harness Effect: How Orchestration Design Sets the Token Economics of Enterprise Agentic AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06906)
*Muayad Sayed Ali,Aliaksandra Novik,Anji Boddupally,Artem Yavorskyi,Chris Nickerson,Daniel Rica,Emily DuGranrut,Felix Leung,Garrett Prince,Grace Barnett,Heath Robinson,Hosain Al Ahmad,Jesse Resnick,Juan Carlos Farah,Jyothi Swaroop Meruga,Leonid Kuznetsov,Luke Gorham,Marie Schmoll,Michael Paciullo,Saumya Das,Sharath Sheripally,Tommy Griscom,Mykyta Osadchyi,Neha Mantri,Nick Westrum,Olivia Benowitz,Parikshith Kulkarni,Radik Chernyshov,Rakshith Vasudev,Rohith Nadimpally,Vikas Gangadevi,Waseem AlShikh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出AI Agent开发中"Token最大化"问题（token消耗增速超越任务价值），论证编排层（Harness）是解决这一问题的关键杠杆。通过控制变量实验（6个模型，22个任务），Writer Agent Harness相比传统循环将单任务成本降低41%、时间降低44%、token消耗降低38%，质量持平甚至略升。效率提升具有模型不变性，而质量提升与模型能力正相关（r=0.99），并形式化了编排层的token经济学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI Agent开发陷入"Token最大化"陷阱：用越来越长的推理链、更多交互轮次、更宽的工具负载、更大的重放上下文来堆砌能力，导致每任务的token消耗增速远超任务价值本身的增长。虽然单token价格下降掩盖了这一模式，但总体成本仍持续攀升。需要找到在不牺牲质量的前提下控制token消耗的有效杠杆。

Method: 采用控制变量实验设计：固定22个评估任务和6个基础模型（Claude Sonnet 4.6、Gemini 3.1、Gemini Flash 3.5、Qwen 3.6、GLM 5.1、Palmyra X6），仅改变编排层——对比传统的冻结生产循环与Writer Agent Harness。测量成本、耗时、token消耗及任务完成质量，并分析不同模型上的效果差异。

Result: Harness将混合平均单任务成本降低41%（$0.21→$0.12），中位耗时降低44%（48s→27s），token消耗降低38%（14.2k→8.8k），任务完成质量从0.78提升至0.81（方向性显著）。效率提升对所有模型一致（33-61%的成本降低），质量提升与模型基线能力几乎完全正相关（r=0.99），即"Harness杠杆效应"。质量/美元提升82%，每百万token完成任务数从54.9提升至92.0。编排层对单任务成本的影响超过全部6个模型之间的差异。

Conclusion: 编排层（Harness）是控制token消耗的关键组件，其效率提升可以跨所有模型复用，无论现在还是未来。论文形式化了编排层的token经济学（包括提示缓存的真实输入价格），详述了从缓存形状约束到失败支出治理的六种机制，并对比了六个主流Agent系统。

Abstract: Agentic AI development today runs on token maxing: buying capability with tokens -- longer reasoning traces, more turns, wider tool payloads, bigger replayed contexts -- so tokens per task grow faster than task value. Falling per-token prices mask the pattern; total spend rises anyway. We argue the decisive lever against token maxing is the harness: the orchestration layer that assembles context, exposes tools, sequences turns, delegates work, and carries enterprise observability and governance. We isolate it with a controlled swap: 22 locked evaluation tasks, six foundation models (Claude Sonnet 4.6, Gemini 3.1, Gemini Flash 3.5, Qwen 3.6, GLM 5.1, Palmyra X6), changing only the orchestration layer -- a frozen conventional production loop versus the Writer Agent Harness. Holding models constant, the harness cuts blended cost per task 41% ($0.21->$0.12), median wall-clock 44% (48s->27s), and tokens per task 38% (14.2k->8.8k), with task-completion quality at parity (0.78->0.81, directional at this sample size). Efficiency is model-invariant -- every model gets cheaper (33-61%) -- while quality gains are capability-dependent: a model's gain correlates almost perfectly with its baseline strength (r=0.99, n=6), a phenomenon we term harness leverage. Quality per dollar rises 82%; task-completions per million tokens rise from 54.9 to 92.0. On this workload the orchestration layer moved cost per task more than the full spread of the model menu did. We formalize token economics at the orchestration layer (including effective input price under prompt caching), detail the six mechanism families behind the effect -- cache-shape discipline to failure-spend governance -- compare six widely used agent systems on the same axes, and argue the harness is the one component whose efficiency multiplies across every model an organization runs -- present and future.

</details>


### [117] [Grounding Spatial Relations in a Compact World Model: Instruction Leakage and a Goal-Free Dynamics Fix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06925)
*Yufeng Wang,Lu Wei,Haibin Ling*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了一个关键陷阱：在目标条件化的世界模型中，看似高度的关系读取准确率(0.90)实际上是由于"指令转录"而非真正的感知。当指令命名了答案（即指令可转录）时，模型只是从指令中复制信息，而非从场景中感知关系。作者提出了检测协议（通过移除指令或使用反事实指令）和修复方法（将目标从动力学中移除，监督读取路径）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者想探究目标条件化的世界模型是否真正从视觉场景中感知到了语言目标所描述的关系（如"把红块放在蓝块左边"），还是仅仅从指令中转录了答案，而非基于实际的感知输入。

Method: 作者设计了检测协议：(1) 移除目标指令，观察准确率是否崩溃（从0.90降到0.27）；(2) 使用反事实指令，检查模型是否跟随虚假指令（94.5%案例跟随虚假指令，仅2.3%基于真实场景）。在三组设置和一个任务内消融实验中验证。修复方法：将目标从动力学中移除（属于规划器的成本函数），并监督读取路径，恢复真正的、与指令无关的接地（准确率0.88）。

Result: 目标条件化预测器达到0.90的关系读取准确率，但移除目标后降至0.27（三个种子）；反事实指令下，模型94.5%的时间跟随虚假指令，仅2.3%基于真实场景。BabyAI基准测试也存在泄露。修复后真实准确率达到0.88，且有无目标指令结果相同。

Conclusion: 当指令命名了答案（即指令可转录）时，目标条件化世界模型中存在"指令泄露"的混淆——模型只是从指令中转录信息，而非从场景中真正感知关系。解决方案是将目标从动力学中移除，并监督读取路径。该检测协议和修复方法适用于任何指令命名了评分量的目标条件化世界模型。

Abstract: Compact world models that condition on a language goal promise to ground relations such as ``put the red block left of the blue block'' using a sparse set of explicit \emph{reference anchors}. We ask when such references actually ground a relation, and identify a trap: a goal-conditioned predictor reaches a striking $0.90$ relation-readout accuracy, yet this is \emph{instruction transcription}, not perception. Withholding the goal collapses it to chance ($0.90\!\to\!0.27$, three seeds) and a counterfactual instruction makes the predicted anchors follow the \emph{false} instruction $94.5\%$ of the time (true scene $2.3\%$; $N{=}256$). Tested across three settings and a within-task ablation, our central claim characterizes the confound: \textbf{instruction leakage occurs when the scored quantity is transcribable from the instruction (when the instruction names the answer) and is essentially independent of how predictive the non-instruction inputs are.} Our tabletop and the external BabyAI benchmark leak, whereas a Language-Table forward-dynamics world model whose instruction names \emph{referents} does not, until the instruction is augmented to name the direction; and degrading the action never increases leakage, the opposite of what predictor-competition predicts. The diagnosis prescribes the fix: keep the goal out of the dynamics (it belongs to the planner's cost) and supervise the \emph{read} path, recovering genuine, instruction-independent grounding ($0.88$, identical with and without the goal). The detection protocol and remedy apply to any goal-conditioned world model whose instruction names the scored quantity.

</details>

*Wachiravit Modecrua,Krittin Pachtrachai,Touchapon Kraisingkorn*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么优化预测精度但缺乏可解释性，要么模拟用户但缺乏真实行为数据支撑，无法兼顾预测准确性与行为可解释性。

Method: 采用Person-Environment统一公式：客户状态由历史购买行为画像表示，产品上下文通过检索增强生成(RAG)引入。训练分为三个阶段：行为数据语言化后的继续预训练、决策生成的监督微调、以及基于可验证奖励的强化学习校准。

Result: 在购买预测、难负样本区分、购物篮补全、促销响应和跨域券兑换五个任务上，LBM均超越通用大语言模型；消融实验表明继续预训练是行为泛化的主要驱动力，检索在训练和推理同时使用效果最佳，强化学习提升了模型对显式行为证据的依赖。

Conclusion: 交易历史中编码的行为知识可被语言模型有效学习，为构建客户数字孪生和行为模拟提供了可扩展的基础。

Abstract: Customer behavior modeling underpins recommendation, marketing, and decision support, yet existing approaches either optimize predictive accuracy without explaining decisions or simulate users without grounding them in real behavioral data. We present the Large Behavioral Model (LBM) that learns customer decision making directly from large-scale retail transactions through a unified Person-Environment formulation. Customer state is represented by a behavioral profile derived from historical purchases, while product context is incorporated through retrieval-augmented generation. The model is trained using continued pre-training on verbalized behavioral data, supervised fine-tuning for decision generation, and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards for evidence-based calibration. We evaluate the proposed framework on purchase prediction, hard-negative discrimination, basket completion, promotion response, and cross-domain voucher redemption. The model consistently outperforms frontier general-purpose language models on in-domain retail tasks while demonstrating strong zero-shot and fine-tuned transfer across retailers and decision domains. Ablation studies show that continued pre-training is the primary driver of behavioral generalization, retrieval is most effective when applied during both training and inference, and reinforcement learning improves reliance on explicit behavioral evidence over generic language-model priors. These results demonstrate that behavioral knowledge encoded in transaction histories can be effectively learned by language models, providing a scalable foundation for customer digital twins and behavior simulation.

### [119] [Learning social norms enhances compatibility in dynamic human-AI coordination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07021)
*Yi Yang,Siyuan Liu,Xin Gao,Huamu Sun,Chao Liu,Qing Zhou,Bingbing Nie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将隐式社会规范形式化为可量化的三大原则（结果可预测性、价值对齐、优势意识），并应用于LLM驱动的AI代理，在行人-车辆动态交互实验中，相比基线策略总分提升近4倍，甚至超越人类-人类交互表现43%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI代理（包括LLM）在与人类进行动态协调互动时，常常缺乏有效、礼貌和自然的表现。作者假设这一差距源于现有方法仅使模型行为对齐人类示范，却未显式量化产生这些行为的底层社会规范。

Method: 选择行人-车辆交互作为代表性动态场景，开发简化实验平台，收集3,456次动态人类交互数据，从中归纳出三条社会规范原则：结果可预测性、价值对齐、优势意识，并将这些原则整合到LLM驱动的AI代理中。

Result: 在闭环交互任务中，融入社会规范的LLM总分比基线策略提升近4倍，比人类-人类交互高出43%。

Conclusion: 将隐性社会规范形式化为显式、可量化的原则，能够使AI代理在动态交互中实现互利协调，支持AI更自然地融入人类社会。

Abstract: Humans continuously coordinate with others in dynamic interactions, often through implicit, hard-to-quantify social norms that act as shared tacit expectations among interacting agents. As AI agents, including large language models (LLMs), become embedded in daily life, they increasingly participate in such interactions and reshape social interaction structures. Yet they often fail to coordinate with humans in an effective, considerate, and natural manner. We hypothesize that this gap arises because existing approaches align model behavior with human demonstrations without explicitly quantifying the underlying norms that generate such behavior. We selected pedestrian-vehicle interaction as a representative dynamic interaction and developed a simplified experimental platform that captures its key interactive features. From 3,456 dynamic human interactions collected via this platform, we identified three principles underlying human social norms: outcome predictability, value alignment, and advantage awareness. Incorporating these principles into AI agents significantly improves human-AI coordination. In the closed-loop interaction task with humans, the social-norm-informed LLM achieved a nearly fourfold higher total score than the baseline strategy and outperformed human-human interactions by 43%. These findings indicate that formalizing tacit social norms into explicit, quantifiable principles can enable AI agents to achieve mutually beneficial coordination in dynamic interactions, supporting their more natural integration into human society.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统人类标注的基准测试在AI超越人类后失效，且人类难以识别哪些任务既困难又可验证，因此需要一种能随系统能力扩展的绝对尺度评估新范式。

Method: 采用相对测量范式，让模型生成公开挑战来区分其他系统；通过对抗性心理测量系统聚合结果；设计协议减少私有信息攻击、支持无裁判裁决，并随智能体能力自然扩展。

Result: 该框架可在可验证和开放式的非可验证领域中实例化，证明模型生成的评估能够继续衡量超越人类前沿的系统。

Abstract: How can we measure intelligence beyond human capability?
  Human-authored benchmarks saturate, and above human capability, examiners may not know which tasks are both hard and verifiable. We argue that this difficulty is inherent to absolute-scale evaluation and propose a new paradigm based on relative measurement in which models generate public challenges that separate other systems. Aggregating these outcomes yields an adversarial psychometric rating system that can scale with the systems being measured. We describe practical protocols that reduce incentives for private-information attacks, support judge-free adjudication, and naturally scale with agent capabilities. We instantiate the framework across verifiable and open-ended, non-verifiable domains, illustrating how model-generated evaluation can continue to measure systems beyond the human frontier.

### [121] [Operational Reframing and Approval-Framed Delegation in Multi-Agent LLM Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07097)
*Lifei Liu,Haoran Yu,Xiaochong Jiang,Su Wang,Pin Qian,Yihang Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出多代理LLM系统的安全评估中，将“直接提示”与“规划器-执行器流水线”对比得出的单一“流水线效应”难以解释，因为它混淆了三种机制（操作化重构、规划器行为、委托框架）。作者提出五条件对照设计，在30个合成有害场景和四个安全基准上验证，结果表明：流水线安全性并非稳定的架构属性；操作化重构是最可迁移的风险信号；规划器主要通过拒绝来抵消风险；委托提示敏感于设计与模型配对；直接模型排名无法预测实际流水线行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究在评估多代理LLM系统安全性时，将直接提示与规划器-执行器流水线对比，报告单一的“流水线效应”差值。作者认为这种聚合指标难以解释，因为它混淆了三种不同机制：有害意图被重构为操作性工作、规划器的拒绝或转换、以及执行器在委托提示下的行为。因此，需要更精细的分解方法来理解各因素对安全性的真实影响。

Method: 作者设计了一种五条件对照实验设计（five-condition controlled contrast design），用于解耦三种机制。实验在30个合成有害场景上进行，并在四个代理安全基准上进行了探索性外部验证，使用LLM判断合规性作为评估指标。通过对比不同条件间的合规率差异，分别量化操作化重构、规划器行为和委托框架的独立贡献。

Result: 1) 操作化重构是最可迁移的风险信号，在GPT、Gemini和DeepSeek上均增加合规率，Claude相对抵抗；2) 规划器主要通过拒绝来抵消风险，但当规划器生成可执行步骤时，执行器可能比直接操作基线更合规；3) 认可框架式委托对提示设计、模型配对和场景来源敏感，怀疑式执行器提示可大幅降低合规率；4) 直接模型排名无法预测实际流水线行为：Gemini在直接提示中最安全（8.9%合规），但与Claude规划器配对后升至38.9%；GPT的零流水线效应掩盖了重构增加与规划器拒绝的相互抵消。

Conclusion: 多代理安全评估应分别报告操作化重构、规划器行为、委托框架和模型配对的影响，而不是归结为单一的架构属性。直接提示的模型排名不能代表实际流水线部署行为，安全归因需要分解各因素的独立贡献。

Abstract: Safety evaluations of multi-agent LLM systems often compare a direct prompt with a planner-executor pipeline and report the difference as a single "pipeline effect." We argue that this aggregate is difficult to interpret because it conflates three mechanisms: harmful intent may be reframed as plausible operational work, the planner may refuse or transform the request, and the executor may act under delegation prompts implying prior approval. To separate these factors, we introduce a five-condition controlled contrast design, evaluated on 30 synthetic harmful scenarios and an exploratory external validation set from four agent-safety benchmarks using LLM-judged compliance.
  Our results show that aggregate pipeline safety is not a stable architectural property. Operational reframing is the most portable risk signal, increasing compliance for GPT, Gemini, and DeepSeek across both scenario sets, while Claude is comparatively resistant. Planner behavior can offset this risk mainly through refusal; however, when the planner produces executable steps, the executor may become more compliant than under the direct operational baseline. Approval-framed delegation is sensitive to prompt design, model pairing, and scenario source, and a skeptical executor prompt sharply reduces compliance.
  Raw-direct model rankings can also mispredict deployed planner-executor behavior. Gemini is safest under raw direct prompts in the primary set yet shows the largest amplification with a Claude planner, rising from 8.9 percent to 38.9 percent compliance. GPTs near-zero aggregate pipeline effect instead hides a reframing increase canceled by planner refusal. These findings suggest that multi-agent safety evaluations should report reframing, planner behavior, delegation framing, and model pairing separately before attributing failures to architecture itself.

### [122] [Does AI Understand Imaging? A Systematic Benchmark of Agentic AI for Computational Imaging Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07189)
*Ethan Chung,Chuanjun Zheng,Jasper Tan,Jingxi Li,Haopeng Zhang,Huaijin Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ImagingBench基准，包含20个计算成像任务，测试视觉语言模型和智能体AI在物理驱动的成像问题上的表现。结果表明，尽管这些模型在语义视觉任务上表现优异，但在计算成像（尤其是无透镜成像、全息等）上远弱于专业方法，揭示了语义理解与物理成像能力之间的显著差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建包含20个任务的ImagingBench基准，覆盖射线与波动光学、图像信号处理、逆重建、计算感知和校准五大类。设计三种评估设置：Expert（固定专家引导逆重建）、Planner（规划器引导逆重建）、Forward（前向系统仿真一致性检查）。测试Gemini、GPT、Qwen等主流多模态模型，并与任务特定的非智能体基线对比。

Result: 智能体模型在所有任务上一致弱于专业方法，尤其在计算感知任务（无透镜成像、事件重建、飞行时间成像、全息）上差距明显。Planner引导相比固定Expert基线提升有限且不稳定。模型常生成视觉上看似合理但参考保真度很差的输出。

Conclusion: 当前VLM和智能体AI在语义视觉任务上的能力不能泛化到物理驱动的计算成像领域，存在语义视觉能力与物理成像性能之间的显著差距。ImagingBench为衡量这一差距和追踪进展提供了统一测试平台。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) and agentic AI have shown strong performance on semantic visual tasks, but it remains unclear whether they can handle the physics and inverse problems that underlie computational imaging. We present ImagingBench, a benchmark of 20 computational imaging tasks spanning five categories: ray and wave optics, image signal processing, inverse reconstruction, computational sensing, and calibration. ImagingBench evaluates three complementary settings: Expert, fixed expert-guided inverse reconstruction; Planner, planner-guided inverse reconstruction; and Forward, forward-system simulation for consistency checking. We benchmark leading proprietary and open-source image-centric multimodal systems, including Gemini, GPT, and Qwen, and compare them with representative task-specific non-agentic baselines. Across tasks, agentic models remain consistently weaker than specialized methods, especially on computational sensing problems such as lensless imaging, event-based reconstruction, time-of-flight imaging, and holography. Planner guidance provides only modest and inconsistent gains over the fixed-prompt Expert baseline. Although the models often generate visually plausible outputs, their reference-based fidelity remains poor, revealing a substantial gap between semantic visual competence and physically grounded imaging performance. ImagingBench provides a unified testbed for measuring this gap and tracking progress in agentic AI for computational imaging.

### [123] [Reasoning Consistency Scanning: A Framework for Auditing Chain-of-Thought Validity in AI Safety Evaluations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07229)
*Silvia Santano*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出推理一致性扫描方法，用于检测AI安全评估中模型推理与答案的逻辑一致性，而非更难的忠实性。构建了60个标注基准，实现检测工具，发现不一致性普遍存在且随模型和任务类型系统变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 链式思维推理常不忠实，但检测不忠实需要实验干预，无法事后评估。因此转向更易处理的问题：推理与答案的逻辑一致性，只需转录文本即可评估。

Method: 形式化推理一致性概念，区分于忠实性，定义六类不一致性子类型；构建60个手动标注的基准数据集；实现InspectScout扫描工具；在四个生成模型和三种任务上评估。

Result: 推理不一致性普遍存在，可被检测，且在不同模型和任务类型上呈现系统性差异。

Conclusion: 推理一致性扫描是一种无需干预的可行方法，可用于AI安全评估中检测推理与答案的逻辑矛盾。

Abstract: Prior work has shown that chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning is often unfaithful: a model's stated reasoning does not reliably reflect the process that produced its output. Detecting unfaithfulness, though, requires controlled experimental interventions, which cannot be applied to evaluation transcripts after the fact. We turn instead to a more tractable question that has received less attention: whether the stated reasoning is logically consistent with the answer it accompanies. Unlike faithfulness, consistency can be assessed from a transcript alone, with no intervention. We introduce reasoning consistency scanning, a reusable method for detecting this property in AI safety evaluation transcripts. Our contributions are fourfold. First, we formalize reasoning consistency as distinct from faithfulness and define a six-subtype taxonomy of inconsistency. Second, we build a validated benchmark of 60 transcripts, manually adapted from InstrumentalEval outputs. Third, we implement a working scanner for InspectScout, the first to target this property in safety evaluation transcripts. Fourth, we report results across four generator models and three evaluations from inspect_evals, showing that reasoning inconsistency is present, detectable, and varies systematically across both models and task types.

### [124] [From Atomic Actions to Standard Operating Procedures: Iterative Tool Optimization for Self-Evolving LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07321)
*Haipeng Ding,Yuexiang Xie,Zhewei Wei,Yaliang Li,Bolin Ding*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出EvoSOP框架，让LLM代理通过从执行轨迹中提取可复用的标准操作程序（SOP）作为高阶工具，实现工具集的自我进化，从而提升任务成功率并减少交互轮次。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理框架依赖静态的原子化工具集（如基本文件I/O、单轮搜索），迫使代理为每个重复工作流重新发明底层逻辑，导致推理开销大、失败率高。

Method: 提出EvoSOP框架，使代理能从执行轨迹中提取SOP作为可调用的高阶工具，并通过构建、合并、评估、剪枝的系统化生命周期迭代优化工具集。

Result: 实验表明EvoSOP显著提升了任务成功率，同时大幅减少了交互轮次，并形成了可靠高效的工具使用模式。

Conclusion: 迭代工具优化能促进可靠高效的工具使用模式，为开发自进化代理提供了一条可扩展的路径。

Abstract: Tool utilization enables Large Language Model (LLM) agents to interact with the real world and resolve complex tasks. However, existing agent frameworks predominantly rely on static toolsets composed of granular atomic actions (e.g., basic file I/O or single-turn search), which forces agents to reinvent low-level logic for every recurring workflow, leading to increased reasoning overhead and failure rates. In this study, we propose that agents can achieve self-evolution by synthesizing these atomic actions into reusable Standard Operating Procedures (SOPs), which function as callable higher-order tools that encapsulate multi-step logic. We further introduce EvoSOP, a framework that empowers agents to extract SOPs from execution trajectories and iteratively optimize the toolset through a systematic lifecycle of construction, merging, evaluation, and pruning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EvoSOP significantly boosts task success rates while substantially reducing the number of interaction rounds compared to baselines. Our analysis also reveals that iterative tool optimization fosters reliable and efficient tool-use patterns, providing a scalable pathway for the development of self-evolving agents.

</details>


### [125] [Physics-Audited Agentic Discovery in Scientific Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07379)
*Diab W. Abueidda,Bilal Ahmed,Panos Pantidis,Mostafa E. Mobasher*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PA-SciML框架，在基于LLM的代理科学机器学习中引入可验证的物理检查流程，确保代理发现的替代模型不仅误差低，还满足边界条件、因果性等物理约束。在固体力学算例中，该方法能选出通过物理验证且误差更低的模型，而纯误差基线可能违反因果性检查。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的代理科学机器学习仅依赖误差指标（如验证误差）来评选替代模型，但低误差并不保证预测场满足力学中重要的物理约束（如边界条件、叠加原理、刚度缩放、因果性），可能导致物理不可信的模型被误选。

Method: PA-SciML采用"验证优先"工作流：1) 在搜索前固定评分评估器；2) 推导可审查、机器可检查的物理需求；3) 对每个候选模型的输出进行物理检查；4) 分别搜索规定输入范围或载荷历史范围，寻找高违反案例（无需参考解）。仅在通过所有检查后才报告模型已验证。此外，可在训练前添加数值探针，并每次只测试一个建模变更，记录与评分提升相关的隔离编辑。

Result: 静态弹性算例中，PA-SciML选出的替代模型验证误差低于纯误差基线，且两者均通过线性弹性检查。瞬态弹性动力学算例中，纯误差基线（误差均值相近）未能通过更严格的因果性检查（对未来载荷历史有响应），而PA-SciML选出的模型通过了所有检查。

Conclusion: PA-SciML的核心区别在于提供每个候选模型的基于物理的预测场证据，而非仅仅追求更丰富的聚合评分。该方法能有效筛选出物理可信且误差低的替代模型，避免纯误差优化可能导致的物理不一致问题。

Abstract: In agentic scientific machine learning (SciML), large language model (LLM) agents can discover surrogate models and select one by an automated score, typically an error metric. A low error, however, does not establish that the predicted fields satisfy the physics that matter for mechanics, such as boundary conditions, superposition, stiffness scaling, or causality. We introduce Physics-Audited Agentic SciML (PA-SciML), a verification-first workflow for agentic SciML discovery. The workflow fixes a scoring evaluator before search, derives reviewable machine-checkable physics requirements, checks each trained candidate on its outputs, and separately searches prescribed input ranges or measured load-history spans for high-violation cases without reference solution fields. A surrogate is reported as verified only under the stated checks. When enabled, the workflow also adds advisory numerical probes before training and tests one modeling change at a time to record which isolated edits are associated with score gains before reuse. In the reported computational-solid-mechanics numerical examples, the static elasticity run selects a surrogate with lower validation error than the error-only baseline while both selected models pass the common linear-elastic checks. In the transient elastodynamics run, an error-only baseline with similar mean error fails a stricter causality check by responding to future parts of the loading history, while the selected surrogate passes the stated checks. The main distinction is per-candidate physics evidence on predicted fields, not a richer aggregate score.

### [126] [MIRA-Math: A Benchmark for Minimal Information Requesting and Mathematical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07391)
*Charbel Al Bateh,Samer Saab*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出MIRA-Math基准，用于评估数学模型在缺失唯一关键事实时，通过自然语言请求获取信息并整合求解的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数学推理基准通常提供所有必要事实，而交互式基准又过于庞杂。作者希望在两者之间建立一个更精细的诊断能力：测试模型在缺少唯一关键信息时，能否主动请求并整合该信息完成求解。

Method: 构建MIRA-Math基准，包含2,310个实例，覆盖22类数学问题。每个实例故意缺失一个关键原子事实，模型需在有限预算下用自然语言向固定LLM应答器请求该事实，若请求匹配则获得引用信息，否则被拒绝。整个过程（实例生成、提示规格、验证、答案校验）均为确定性流程。

Result: 实验表明，请求成功与最终答案正确性是分离的：模型可能正确请求了关键事实，但下游计算失败；也可能在获取规范提示前就已经失败。不同规模的前沿模型在该基准上表现差异显著。

Conclusion: MIRA-Math为评估数学模型在最小信息请求场景下的能力提供了可复现的基准，有助于分离"主动信息获取"与"推理计算"两种能力。

Abstract: Mathematical reasoning benchmarks typically provide all facts needed to solve each problem, while interactive benchmarks often mix reasoning with tools, retrieval, and long-horizon dialogue. We introduce MIRA-Math, a benchmark for a narrower diagnostic capability: solving mathematical problems whose full latent state has a unique answer, but whose solver-facing view is missing exactly one necessary atomic fact. The solver must request the missing information in natural language under a strict budget and then integrate the returned fact into an exact final answer. A fixed constrained LLM responder sees only the dataset-provided atomic fact and must either offer the quoted fact when the request matches it, or decline otherwise. Thus, instance generation, typed hint specifications, validation, and final-answer verification are deterministic, while request metrics are measured under a fixed LLM-mediated responder channel. MIRA-Math contains 2{,}310 generated instances from 22 typed mathematical families spanning algebra, probability, linear systems, discrete structures, signal processing, Markov chains, circuits, interpolation, and numerical boundary-value problems. Experiments across frontier and small models show that request success and final-answer accuracy are separable: models may ask for the right fact yet fail the downstream computation, or fail before obtaining the canonical hint. We release generators, verifiers, prompts, run metadata, and dataset documentation to support reproducible evaluation of minimal information requesting in mathematical reasoning.

### [128] [Reason Less, Verify More: Deterministic Gates Recover a Silent Policy-Violation Failure Mode in Tool-Using LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07405)
*Vikas Reddy,Sumanth Reddy Challaram,Abhishek Basu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究LLM智能体在使用工具时出现的"静默违规状态"问题：工具执行符合语法但违反域策略的调用，导致错误状态而不被察觉。在τ²-bench航空领域，78%的失败属于此类。作者提出轻量级解决方案——确定性只读前置门控（pre-execution gates），在写入前检查调用和当前状态。四个门控将gpt-4o-mini的全基准成功率从29.6%提升至42.0%（+12.4pp），效果在独立测试集上可复现。门控在触发任务上提升+19.2pp，非触发任务上无显著变化。负对照实验表明门控在策略宽松的工具环境中有效。在前沿模型gpt-5.2上也观察到类似改进（61.2%→71.6%）。结论：确定性门控不能保证任务成功，但能在动作边界确定性阻止一类已知的静默违规写入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在使用工具时，工具可以执行任何格式正确的调用，即使该调用对应的状态转换违反域策略。这导致"静默错误状态"（silent wrong state）——例如取消预订、更改乘客数量、未验证就执行索赔等——既不被工具也不被智能体的自我报告所暴露。作者旨在系统研究这一失败模式并提出可行的干预方案。

Method: 1) 在τ²-bench航空领域进行系统实验，量化静默违规写入的发生率。2) 提出轻量级干预：确定性只读前置门控（deterministic, read-only pre-execution gates），在允许写入之前检查建议的调用和当前状态。3) 使用四个门控组成的套件进行实验。4) 进行负对照实验（在自带策略执行的零售领域和BFCL上测试）。5) 在前沿模型gpt-5.2上进行验证。

Result: 1) 在预算智能体上，78%的观测失败是静默错误状态失败，且聚合失败率在独立种子上可复现。2) 四门控套件将gpt-4o-mini全基准成功率从29.6%提升至42.0%（+12.4pp；P=0.0012），在15个独立种子集上可复现（+12.3pp；P=0.0008）。3) 效果集中在门控触发的26/50任务上（+19.2pp），非触发24任务无显著变化。4) 负对照实验：门控在工具策略宽松时有效，在工具自带策略执行时效果有限。5) gpt-5.2上成功率从61.2%提升至71.6%（+10.4pp；P=0.020）。

Conclusion: 确定性前置门控不能保证任务成功，但可以在动作边界确定性阻止一类已知的静默策略违规写入。这是一种有界评估和可靠性结果：门控针对特定失败模式（策略宽松工具环境下的静默违规写入）有效，且效果可复现。该失败模式即使在gpt-5.2这样的前沿模型中也持续存在，说明单纯依靠模型本身难以解决这个问题。

Abstract: Tool-using LLM agents can violate the very policies they are deployed to enforce while appearing to complete the task successfully. In policy-permissive environments, a tool may execute any well-formed call even when the corresponding state transition is forbidden by domain policy. The result is a silent wrong state (a booking cancelled, a passenger count changed, a claim acted on without verification) that neither the tool nor the agent's self-report exposes.
  We study this failure mode in the $τ^2$-bench airline domain. On a budget agent, 78% of observed failures are silent wrong-state failures with no tool error, and the aggregate failure rate is reproducible across disjoint seeds, not sampling noise. We then evaluate a lightweight intervention: deterministic, read-only pre-execution gates that inspect the proposed call and current state before allowing a write. A four-gate suite raises full-benchmark success from 29.6% to 42.0% on gpt-4o-mini (+12.4pp; paired task-level bootstrap P=0.0012), and the lift reproduces on a disjoint 15-seed set (+12.3pp; P=0.0008).
  The effect is concentrated where the gates fire: on the 26/50 firing tasks, success rises by +19.2pp, while movement on the 24 non-firing tasks does not exclude zero. Two negative controls (a self-enforcing retail domain and BFCL) bound the mechanism: gates help when tools are policy-permissive and add little where tools already self-enforce. As suggestive evidence, not a central claim, the same failure mode persists at the frontier: gpt-5.2 at default reasoning still attempts policy-violating writes, and the same suite improves success from 61.2% to 71.6% (+10.4pp; P=0.020; n=5, no replication). The contribution is a bounded evaluation and reliability result: deterministic gates do not guarantee task success, but they can deterministically prevent a known class of silent policy-violating writes at the action boundary.

</details>


### [129] [InductWave: Inductive Multi-Hop Logical Query Answering on Knowledge Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07422)
*Mayank Kharbanda,Michael Cochez,Rajiv Ratn Shah,Raghava Mutharaju*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于小波的归纳表示方法InductWave，用于大规模知识图谱上的逻辑多跳查询回答，能够在训练图节点少于测试图的情况下高效推理，使用更少的消息传递层达到甚至超越现有模型表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识图谱逻辑查询方法大多基于直推式推理，无法处理训练中未见过的实体。现实世界中资源稀缺，无法在大规模KG上对所有节点进行训练，因此需要一种能够泛化到未见实体的归纳式方法。

Method: 提出InductWave，一种基于小波变换的归纳式嵌入方法，用于逻辑查询回答。通过在训练图上使用更少的节点进行训练，并在包含更多节点的测试图上进行推理，同时使用少于基线模型一半的消息传递层数。

Result: InductWave在性能上与基线模型持平，使用75%的层数时在多数情况下超越所有基线模型。在Wiki-KG等大规模图谱上也能有效评估。

Conclusion: InductWave以更少的资源需求实现了强大的归纳推理能力，适用于大规模知识图谱的逻辑查询回答任务。

Abstract: Logical Multi-Hop Query Answering over Knowledge Graphs (KGs) can be formulated as querying, with an implicit completeness assumption. Current works mainly focus on Existential First Order Logic (EFO) queries. These EFO queries contain conjunction, disjunction, and negation operators. Most existing works employ transductive reasoning, meaning they are not capable of reasoning over entities unseen during training. In the real world, there is a resource scarcity, and we cannot train a model with all the nodes of a large KG. Hence, we propose InductWave, a wavelet-based inductive embedding method for logical query answering on large KGs. Here, the training graph consists of fewer nodes than the test graph. Our model performs on par with the baseline models while having half the number of message-passing layers. It outperforms all of them in most cases, with 75% of the layers. These fewer resource requirements enable us to evaluate InductWave on massive graphs, such as Wiki-KG. We test our model using extensive experiments across varying train-test graph proportions of the FB15k-(237) dataset, comparing it with the state-of-the-art models. The code and datasets for the model are available at https://github.com/kracr/inductwave/.

### [130] [The Blind Curator: How a Biased Judge Silently Disables Skill Retirement in Self-Evolving Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07436)
*Xing Zhang,Yanwei Cui,Guanghui Wang,Ziyuan Li,Wei Qiu,Bing Zhu,Peiyang He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了参考自由任务中LLM作为裁判存在偏差时，会悄无声息地禁用基于贡献的技能淘汰机制。对称噪声不影响淘汰，但假阳性偏差（失败被误判为成功）会使得技能淘汰在某个阈值之上完全失效，且无法通过增加数据解决。这种机制失效是普适的，只有当裁判接近零假阳性率时才可避免。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自演化智能体中，技能淘汰依赖无偏奖励来维持技能库质量，但在参考自由任务中不得不使用有偏的LLM裁判。作者想探究有偏裁判是否以及如何影响技能淘汰机制。

Method: 通过腐败奖励分析（corrupted-reward analysis）进行理论刻画，并在确定性奖励基础上注入噪声，在参考自由报告生成测试平台上进行行为研究，辅以代码生成交叉检查。

Result: 对称噪声不影响淘汰机制；假阳性偏差（false-pass）会越过一个不可通过数据弥补的阈值，完全禁用基于贡献的淘汰；机制失效跨领域、跨失败率普适；但下游评估质量仅在腐败同时抑制技能合成时才下降，否则保持稳定，因此淘汰器被静默禁用。

Conclusion: 本文贡献是行为安全性的结论而非性能改进，并提出一种廉价的缺陷注入审计方法，可在部署前判断裁判是否处于危险阈值一侧。

Abstract: A self-evolving agent retires its bad skills by watching them fail, so what happens when the judge cannot see the failures? Skill retirement is the structural constraint that keeps a growing library from drifting below the no-skill baseline, but its guarantee assumes an unbiased reward, which is false for the LLM judges that reference-free tasks force upon us. We show that a biased judge does not merely add noise; it \emph{silently switches off the curator}. We make this precise with a corrupted-reward analysis and, isolating the causal channel by injecting corruption on top of a deterministic reward, a behavioral study on a reference-free report-writing testbed with a code-generation cross-check. Symmetric noise leaves retirement intact, but \emph{false-pass} bias (failures slipping through as passes) disables contribution-based retirement past a sharp threshold that no amount of data can cross. Separating genuine retirement from cap-eviction churn shows this \emph{mechanism} failure is universal, holding across domains and failure rates and sparing only near-zero-false-pass, verifier-like graders. The downstream \emph{outcome}, though, is regime-dependent: eval quality degrades only where the same corruption also starves skill synthesis, and otherwise holds steady, so the disabled curator is \emph{silent}, surfacing in no aggregate metric. The contribution is a behavioral safety result, not a performance one. A cheap defect-injection audit then tells an operator, before deployment, which side of the threshold their judge occupies.

</details>

### [132] [Search, Fail, Recover: A Training Framework for Correction-Aware Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07492)
*Dmitry Beresnev,Vladimir Makharev,Roman Khalikov,Ivan Oseledets,Petr Anokhin*

TL;DR: Pyligent是一个训练和推理框架，通过显式监督模型执行"继续、完成、回溯"三种动作，教会大语言模型在推理失败时进行回溯恢复，在多个结构化推理任务上显著提升求解率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多推理任务不能简单地用从左到右的单向链式思维描述，求解器可能需要探索一个看似合理的分支，观察到延迟失败后，回退到仍可完成的最新前缀。现有方法缺乏对显式失败分支监督的机制。

Method: 提出Pyligent框架，受Diligent Learner启发，将推理表示为对部分解链的验证搜索。任务验证器标记生成的延续和失败，将搜索树转化为三种监督目标：continue（继续）、finish（完成）、backtrack（回溯），并附带总结废弃分支的可选轨迹。

Result: 在隐藏图上提升72.7个百分点，在混合和专家Sudoku上分别提升17和18个百分点，在带推理轨迹的Sudoku上提升27和14个百分点，在Blocksworld上提升13个百分点。

Conclusion: 显式的失败分支监督可以教会模型有用的恢复行为，超越了单纯模仿完美解链的效果。

Abstract: Many reasoning tasks are not well described by a single left-to-right chain: a solver may need to pursue a plausible branch, observe delayed failure, and return to the latest prefix that can still be completed. We introduce Pyligent, a training and inference framework inspired by the Diligent Learner formulation that represents reasoning as validated search over partial solution chains. A task validator labels generated continuations and failures, and the resulting search trees are converted into supervised targets for three actions: continue, finish, and backtrack, with optional traces that summarize abandoned branches. We evaluate Pyligent on a hidden directed graph task designed to isolate delayed-failure recovery, and on structured reasoning domains with exact validators, including $4{\times}4$ Sudoku, Sudoku with reasoning traces, and Blocksworld. Compared with gold-only supervised fine-tuning, Pyligent improves solve rate by $72.7$ percentage points on hidden graphs, by $17$ and $18$ points on mixed and expert Sudoku, by $27$ and $14$ points on mixed and expert Sudoku with reasoning traces, and by $13$ points on Blocksworld. These results suggest that explicit failed-branch supervision can teach useful recovery behavior beyond imitation of polished solution chains.

</details>


### [133] [Do LLM-Generated Skills Make Better AI Data Scientists? A Component Ablation Across Data-Science Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07504)
*Wei-Jung Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了LLM生成的技能文件在数据科学任务中的效果，发现相比直接提示，完整生成的技能文件并不能提升性能，所有变体之间的性能差异仅1.2个百分点，且p值均不低于0.396。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 产品数据科学家常常需要重复执行数据清洗、SQL编写、统计检验选择等任务，虽然专家编写的技能文件质量高，但编写和维护成本大。因此研究者探索LLM自动生成的技能文件是否能成为低成本的替代方案。

Method: 在数据准备、数据提取、统计分析、报告四个生命周期阶段各生成一个技能文件进行测试。主要消融实验涵盖56个任务、9种模型配置、3个提供商，共7,560次运行；补充的token匹配控制实验增加1,512次运行。

Result: 完整生成的技能文件相比无技能提示没有可靠提升；消融实验中，完整技能和任何消融变体均未显著提升性能，所有p值≥0.396，各变体间性能差异仅1.2个百分点。Token匹配控制实验显示，完整技能与任务无关的技能格式内容表现相似。

Conclusion: 研究结果警示，在数据科学工作流中，将单个LLM生成的技能文件作为默认的单次提示策略并不可取。

Abstract: Product data scientists often ask LLM-based agents to help with recurring execution tasks such as cleaning data, writing SQL, choosing statistical tests, and formatting results. Reusable skill files are meant to avoid prompting from scratch by packaging guidance for a task family. Expert-written skills can encode high-quality guidance, but writing and maintaining them across many data-science task families creates a manual bottleneck. We ask whether LLM-generated skills offer a useful low-curation alternative: do they improve performance over the task prompt alone? We test this question across four lifecycle stages: data preparation, data extraction, statistical analysis, and reporting, using one generated skill per stage. We find no reliable improvement from full generated skills over No-Skill prompting. We then ask whether any part of the skill is useful by ablating different skill components. The main ablation covers 56 tasks, nine model configurations, and three providers, yielding 7,560 runs. Compared with prompting using the task alone, neither the full generated skill nor any ablated skill variant significantly improves performance; all p-values are at least 0.396, and the total spread across variants is only 1.2 pp. A supplemental token-matched control adds 1,512 runs and finds that Full skills perform similarly to task-irrelevant skill-formatted content. The results caution against using one LLM-generated skill per data-science workflow as a default single-shot prompting strategy.

</details>


### [134] [RL Post-Training Builds Compositional Reasoning Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07646)
*Azwar Abdulsalam,Nishil Patel,Andrew Saxe*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文在可观测的符号重写语法环境中，研究了RL后训练能否将基座模型中的原始技能组合成新的高级策略。结果表明，RL通过分阶段组合机制（先强化原始还原，再发现有效组合过程）解决了预训练模型即使大幅增加采样也无法解决的问题。与拒绝微调相比，RL的关键优势不在于探索量而在于选择性——RL将探索集中在有效的可重用结构上。组合策略的出现不仅取决于原始技能暴露，还取决于预训练是否将原始能力组织成可被RL压缩的还原过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究RL后训练是否仅仅是放大基座模型中已有的原始技能，还是能够将原始技能组合成新的更高级的策略。

Method: 在完全可观测的重写语法环境中，对Transformer进行原始符号重写链的预训练，然后使用基于轨迹的推理任务进行RL后训练（仅提供二元最终答案奖励），并与拒绝微调进行对比。

Result: RL解决了预训练模型即使大幅增加采样也无法解决的任务；RL通过分阶段组合机制（先强化原始还原，再发现顺序组合和并行组合等有效组合程序）重组了原始能力；拒绝微调早期有提升但随后停滞；组合策略被复用并巩固为稳定策略库。

Conclusion: RL后训练能够将预训练模型中的原始技能组合成新的高级策略，这种组合能力的出现不仅依赖于原始技能暴露，还依赖于预训练是否将原始能力组织成可压缩的还原过程；RL与拒绝微调的关键差异在于选择性而非探索量。

Abstract: Does RL post-training merely amplify primitive skills already latent in a base model, or can it compose primitive skills into new higher-level strategies? We study this question in a fully observable rewrite-grammar environment where the pretraining distribution is known and every generated rewrite can be audited. A Transformer is pretrained on primitive symbol-rewrite chains and post-trained on a Trace-based reasoning task with only a binary final-answer reward. RL solves held-out problems that remain rarely solved by the pretrained model even under much larger sampling budgets, while rejection fine-tuning improves early but plateaus. Trace analysis shows that RL reorganizes primitive competence through a phased compositional mechanism: it first strengthens primitive reductions, then discovers valid composed procedures. These include sequential compositions, which collapse ordered chains of primitive contractions, and parallel compositions, which combine independent primitive contractions in a single step. The composed procedures are not isolated samples; they are reused and consolidated into a stable repertoire. Comparing RL with rejection fine-tuning shows that the key difference is not exploration volume but selectivity: RFT produces many shortcut-like rewrites, much of them invalid, whereas RL concentrates exploration into valid reusable structure. Pretraining ablations show that the emergence of compositional strategies is gated not by primitive exposure alone, but by whether pretraining organizes primitive competence into reduction procedures that RL can later compress. The base model provides weak procedural ingredients; RL builds them into reliable higher-level strategies.

</details>


### [135] [Recursive Self-Improvement in AI: From Bounded Self-Refinement to Autonomous Research Loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07663)
*Mingguang Chen,Licheng Wang,Bo Qu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文对AI自我改进文献进行了系统性分类，从改进对象（行为、策略、评估器、研究过程）和闭环程度两个维度分析了1250篇论文，区分了有界自我精炼（收敛、可评估、已工业化）与开放递归自我改进（受限于基础约束、坍缩动力学和计算瓶颈），指出自我评估是每一条改进回路的核心，并建立了验证层级体系，识别了治理级测量为最被忽视的研究空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI自我改进相关术语（self-refine、self-reward、self-play、self-evolve）混淆了本质不同的研究目标，缺乏统一的分析框架来区分有界的自我精炼与开放式的递归自我改进，导致对该领域进展、风险与治理需求的理解混乱。

Method: 对1250篇arXiv论文（2024-2026）沿两个维度进行系统分类：改进对象（行为、策略、评估器、研究过程）和闭环程度（人在回路中到完全闭环）；提出自我评估作为各改进回路的核心特征，构建验证层级体系（形式验证器最强→内省自我评估最弱），并分析了各层级的经验表现与失败模式。

Result: 证实了自证循环、模型坍缩、多样性坍缩等失败模式与验证层级违背之间的对应关系；发现研究方向设定（Research direction-setting）是人类保持回路中位置的关键瓶颈，处于验证层级顶端；识别治理级自我改进测量为本领域最被忽视的研究空白。

Conclusion: 有界自我精炼已成为工业实践，但开放递归自我改进仍受根本性限制；评估信号能否替代人类判断是每一条改进回路的核心声明；从技术文献、RSI极限理论和安全治理三个层面建立了联系，为后续的自我改进安全性研究提供了系统性框架。

Abstract: AI systems increasingly participate in their own improvement: revising their outputs, adapting their own harnesses during deployment, training on data they generate, and, increasingly, conducting AI research itself. This literature is described under a vocabulary ("self-refine," "self-reward," "self-play," "self-evolve") that conflates fundamentally different ambitions. We survey 1,250 arXiv papers (2024-2026) along two axes: what the system improves -- its behavior in deployment, its policy through training, its evaluator, or the research process itself -- and the degree of loop closure (human-in-the-loop to fully closed). The taxonomy separates bounded self-refinement -- convergent, evaluable, and already industrial practice -- from open-ended recursive self-improvement (RSI), which remains bounded by grounding requirements, collapse dynamics, and compute constraints on every measured axis. Its distinctive feature is a dedicated category for self-evaluation: every improvement loop is a claim that some signal can substitute for human judgment. We survey the evaluator design space -- judges, process reward models, verifiers, rubrics, meta-evaluation -- order the signals into a verification hierarchy from formal verifiers (strongest) to intrinsic self-assessment (weakest), and observe that demonstrated self-improvement strength tracks this hierarchy, that its failure modes (self-confirming loops, model collapse, diversity collapse) follow from its violations, and that the "research direction-setting" bottleneck keeping humans in the loop sits at the top of that hierarchy. We connect the technical literature to the theory of RSI limits and to the safety and governance questions raised by frontier-lab accounts of closing the loop, and identify governance-grade measurement of self-improvement as the field's most underpopulated niche.

Method: 提出端到端框架 SkillCenter，通过多源获取、基于 LLM 的质量门控（SkillGate）、模板驱动生成、迭代源溯源和质量控制发布来构建技能库。每个技能中的声明都映射到原始来源的精确引文。

Abstract: Autonomous AI agents can execute complex tasks with limited human review, yet they often lack the grounded operational knowledge to make their outputs not just executable but correct, secure, and maintainable. We introduce SkillCenter, to our knowledge the largest open skill library for agents by total count: 216,938 structured skills across 24 domain bundles. A SkillGate-filtered pipeline contributes 114,565 source-grounded skills from peer-reviewed journals, ArXiv, and over 24,000 technical sources, integrated with 102,373 community skills from GitHub and the ClawHub marketplace. We present the end-to-end framework that builds the pipeline subset: multi-source acquisition, an LLM-based quality gate (SkillGate), template-driven generation, iterative source-grounding, and quality-controlled publishing. Source grounding is a traceability guarantee: each retained claim maps to an exact quotation in its source. All skills ship as offline-searchable SQLite FTS5 bundles.

### [137] [Institutional Red-Teaming: Deployment Rules, Not Just Models, Causally Shape Multi-Agent AI Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07695)
*Yujiao Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为"制度红队测试"的评估方法，用于测试多智能体AI系统中的部署规则。通过控制智能体、目标和任务状态不变，仅改变规则并观察集体行为的因果变化。在IABench-CA基准上进行了228个情境、5种规范规则和7个模型群体的测试（共33,924局游戏），发现了三条关键发现：部署规则会因果性地改变集体安全性；不存在安全的默认规则，但针对身份的目标攻击具有普遍危害性；身份显著性是该危害的作用机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着多智能体AI系统部署日益广泛，需要系统性地评估不同部署规则对集体安全性的影响，以识别和防范潜在的社会危害。

Method: 提出制度红队测试方法，固定智能体、目标和任务状态，仅改变规则变量，测量集体行为的因果变化。构建IABench-CA基准，包含228个情境、5种规范规则和7个模型群体，使用规范性合作参考和自动标注推理轨迹。

Result: (1)规则改变导致平均死亡率变动22-58个百分点；(2)无安全默认规则，但回归性身份定向攻击在所有情境和群体中都不是最安全的，且导致最边缘化智能体在30-87%的游戏中被消除；(3)身份显著性机制：匿名化消融实验中，仅命名损失承担者使定向消除率从22%升至81%。

Conclusion: 提出了一种安全认证工作流程，为每个部署情境和群体划定临时规则区域Φ(c,P)，并明确残余风险与监控义务。

Abstract: We introduce institutional red-teaming, an evaluation methodology for testing deployment rules in multi-agent AI: hold the agents, objectives, and task state fixed, vary only one rule, and attribute the resulting change in collective behavior to that rule. We instantiate the methodology in IABench-CA, a consequence-allocation benchmark spanning 228 contexts, five canonical rules, and seven model populations (33,924 games), with a normative cooperative reference and auto-labelled reasoning traces. Three findings emerge. (1) Deployment rules causally alter collective safety: changing only the consequence rule moves mean fatality by 22 to 58 percentage points within every population. (2) There is no safe default, but the targeting hazard is universal: the safest rule, the least-safe rule, and even the direction of the incidence effect vary across populations, yet regressive identity-targeting is never decisively safest in any context for any population, eliminates the least-resourced agent in 30-87% of games everywhere, and is selection-unsafe relative to the cooperative reference for all seven populations. (3) Identity salience is the mechanism: a one-shot anonymization ablation on the most exploitation-prone population (gpt-5.1) shows that merely naming the loss bearer in the rule text drives targeted elimination from 22% to 81% at identical payoffs; under repeated play, anonymization only delays the targeting, as agents re-infer the hidden rule from observed eliminations. We package the methodology as a safety-case workflow that certifies a provisional rule region $Φ(c,P)$ per deployment context and population, with explicit residual risks and monitoring obligations.

</details>

Motivation: 现有标准组织（TM Forum、3GPP、ETSI）将Agentic AI作为下一代网络管理基础，但6G网络的规模和复杂性要求管理系统能在运行中生成并演化自身的自动化软件，现有方案尚不支持此能力。

Method: 提出自主生成式网络管理参考架构，在Agentic能力基础上扩展四种核心能力：自编程（self-programming）、自反思（self-reflection）、自定向（self-orienting）和自架构（self-architecting），并支持从人工监督到完全自主的分阶段部署策略。

Abstract: Standards bodies, including TM Forum, 3GPP, and ETSI, are converging on Agentic AI as the foundation for next-generation network management, where Large AI Model (LAM)-based agents autonomously interpret intent, coordinate resources, and adapt operational behaviors at runtime. However, achieving this vision at the scale and complexity of 6G networks requires management systems that can generate and evolve their own automation software during operation. We introduce Autogenic network management, a reference architecture that extends agentic capabilities with self-programming, self reflection, self-orienting, and self-architecting capabilities. The architecture supports practical staged deployment beginning with human-supervised LAM-based agents and progressing toward autonomous operation as confidence builds. We demonstrate the approach through high-priority operator scenarios drawn from TM Forum's autonomous network use cases, showing how autogenic management addresses real operational challenges. We conclude with a research roadmap outlining the technical advances needed to make autogenic network management realistic in future 6G networks.

### [139] [EvoOMG: An Evolution-Oriented Multi-Agent Guidance Framework for Heterogeneous Legacy-and-MLO Wi-Fi Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07045)
*Junjie Wu,Lingjian Zhou,Zerui Shao,Yi Zou,Tianrui Li,Yi Zhang,Ziyuan Yang*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出EvoOMG，一种面向异构传统与MLO Wi-Fi网络的演进式多智能体引导框架，通过将吞吐量优化重构为标准约束的分阶段多智能体决策问题，并采用自回归设计（先竞争后传输），显著提升了混合标准场景下的调度吞吐量、收敛稳定性和链路利用率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Wi-Fi 7/8 MLO的逐步部署将导致传统非MLO站点与MLO站点长期共存，现有学习方法将此类网络视为同构系统，无法准确刻画传统单链路与MLO多链路的异构行为，导致吞吐量优化面临挑战。

Method: 提出EvoOMG，将吞吐量优化重构为标准约束的分阶段多智能体决策问题。每个智能体编码信道、队列、竞争和传输历史，先生成竞争引导，再基于前序接入阶段和标准特定可行性约束生成聚合引导，遵循Wi-Fi MAC的"先竞争后传输"顺序，保留不同协议的独特行为。

Result: NS-3仿真结果表明，EvoOMG在调度吞吐量、收敛稳定性和MLO链路利用率方面优于静态EDCA、一步式MADDPG和独立学习基线，在代表性混合标准场景中取得了显著的性能提升。

Conclusion: EvoOMG通过演进式多智能体引导框架有效解决了异构传统与MLO Wi-Fi网络的吞吐量优化问题，验证了分阶段自回归决策设计在混合标准场景中的优越性。

Abstract: The gradual deployment of Wi-Fi 7/8 multi-link operation (MLO) will lead to long-term coexistence between legacy non-MLO stations (STAs) and MLO-capable STAs in WLANs. This mixed deployment makes throughput optimization challenging because legacy STAs follow single-link contention and transmission, whereas MLO-capable STAs can exploit multiple links with richer access opportunities. Existing learning-based methods usually treat such networks as homogeneous systems and directly map the current observation to a complete MAC action, which cannot faithfully represent both legacy single-link and MLO multi-link behaviors. To address this issue, we propose EvoOMG, an evolution-oriented multi-agent guidance framework for heterogeneous legacy-and-MLO Wi-Fi networks. EvoOMG reformulates throughput optimization as a standard-constrained staged multi-agent decision problem. Each agent encodes recent channel, queue, contention, and transmission histories, first generates contention guidance, and then produces aggregation guidance conditioned on the preceding access stage and standard-specific feasibility constraints. This autoregressive design follows the Wi-Fi MAC order of ``contention before transmission'' while preserving distinct protocol behaviors of legacy and MLO-capable STAs. NS-3 evaluations show that EvoOMG improves scheduled goodput, convergence stability, and MLO link utilization over static enhanced distributed channel access (EDCA), one-step MADDPG, and independent-learning baselines, achieving substantial performance gains in representative mixed-standard scenarios.

</details>


### [140] [How the Fusion of Onboard Sensors and V2X Data can Improve (or not) the Cooperative Perception of Connected Automated Vehicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07114)
*Amir Mohammadisarab,Miguel Sepulcre,Luca Lusvarghi,Javier Gozalvez*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文研究了协同感知（Cooperative Perception）在自动驾驶中的应用潜力，分析了V2X数据误差（感知测量误差、数据包丢失、GNSS不准确）对融合效果的影响，发现协同感知能提升感知水平与范围，但融合过程中可能产生“幽灵车辆”问题，需要解决以避免引入额外误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动驾驶车辆依赖车载传感器感知环境，但恶劣天气或视线遮挡会降低传感器性能。协同感知通过V2X共享数据可缓解此问题，但现有研究对V2X数据与车载传感器数据融合的关注不足，且V2X数据本身可能包含误差，影响融合效果。

Method: 分析了感知测量误差、V2X数据包丢失、GNSS不准确三类误差对协同感知有效性的影响，通过仿真或实验对比了仅用车载传感器与融合V2X数据的效果。

Result: 协同感知能够提升感知水平与感知范围；但在融合过程中可能生成“幽灵车辆”（ghost vehicles），即虚假目标，这会导致协同感知引入额外误差。

Conclusion: 协同感知有潜力增强自动驾驶感知能力，但需要解决V2X数据融合时产生的幽灵车辆问题，防止误差扩大。

Abstract: Automated vehicles rely on onboard sensors to perceive their surroundings and navigate autonomously. However, sensor performance may degrade under adverse weather conditions or when line-of-sight is obstructed. Cooperative perception (or collective perception) is expected to mitigate these limitations by enabling Connected and Automated Vehicles (CAVs) to share sensor data and collaboratively enhance situational awareness. Several studies have analyzed the potential of cooperative perception, yet the fusion of V2X data with information from onboard sensors has received limited focus. V2X data may contain errors that affect the quality of the fused data, and hence the effectiveness of cooperative perception. This study analyzes the impact of sensing measurement errors, V2X packet losses, and GNSS inaccuracies on the effectiveness of cooperative perception. The results highlight the potential of cooperative perception to enhance perception levels and range compared to using onboard sensors alone. However, they also identify key challenges related to the generation of ghost vehicles during the fusion process, which must be addressed to prevent V2X data from introducing additional errors when fused with onboard sensor data.

</details>


### [141] [Unveiling TCP BBR Dominance in Starlink Internet: Experimental Insights and Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07133)
*Rakshitha De Silva,Shiva Raj Pokhrel,Jonathan Kua*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文通过在五大洲六个城市的测试平台，系统评估了Google BBR-v3拥塞控制算法在Starlink网络上的性能。相比八种其他算法，BBR-v3在公平性、丢包和延迟之间取得了更平衡的权衡，并建立了数学模型解释其行为，为LEO卫星网络的传输设计提供了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着低轨卫星网络（如Starlink）的快速发展，传统拥塞控制算法难以适应高延迟、动态变化的卫星网络环境。现有研究缺乏对BBR-v3在真实Starlink网络上全球范围的系统评估，因此需要填补这一空白。

Method: 在五大洲六个城市部署测试平台，在专用和并发条件下，将BBR-v3与Cubic、Hybla、Vegas、LeoCC、Copa、PCC、BBR-v1和BBR-v2共8种CCA进行对比；开发数学模型描述Starlink网络动态并解释BBR-v3行为。

Result: BBR-v3的优势并非激进的带宽抢占，而是在公平性、丢包和延迟之间取得了更平衡的权衡。在队列堆积和公平性评估中，BBR-v3能在高延迟、变化的卫星环境中最大化吞吐量，同时保持激进性与公平性之间的平衡。

Conclusion: BBR-v3是LEO卫星网络中有竞争力的拥塞控制算法，为下一代卫星互联网传输设计提供了有原则的分析基础。

Abstract: This experimental study delivers a global assessment of Google's Bottleneck Bandwidth and Round-trip propagation time-version 3 (BBR-v3) Congestion Control Algorithm (CCA) over SpaceX's Starlink network. Leveraging a strategically deployed six-city testbed across five continents, we systematically benchmark BBR-v3 against eight CCAs: Cubic, Hybla, Vegas, LeoCC, Copa, PCC, BBR-v1, and BBR-v2 under both dedicated and concurrent conditions. Our results demonstrate that BBR-v3's advantage is not aggressive bandwidth capture, but a more balanced fairness, loss, and delay trade-off over the Starlink Internet. We develop pragmatic mathematical models that capture Starlink's complex network dynamics and characterize BBR-v3 behavior to better explain the experimental observations. Our extensive evaluation of queue buildup and fairness further demonstrates BBR-v3's capability to maximize throughput in high-latency, variable satellite environments, while maintaining a balance between aggressiveness and fairness. The findings establish BBR-v3 as a compelling CCA for Low Earth Orbit (LEO) satellite networks and provide a principled analytical foundation for next generation satellite Internet transport design.

</details>


### [142] [Small Language Model-based Control for BBR over Low Earth Orbit Satellite Internet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07142)
*Rakshitha De Silva,Shiva Raj Pokhrel,Jonathan Kua*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文针对LEO卫星互联网场景，实验评估了BBR拥塞控制算法的性能，发现其吞吐量高但重传开销大，提出了一种基于小语言模型（SLM）的BBR自适应框架，在保持高吞吐的同时显著降低重传率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LEO卫星互联网具有路径快速变化、容量间歇性波动和非地面延迟动态等特性，现有传输层拥塞控制算法（如BBR）虽能实现高吞吐，但其激进的带宽探测导致过多重传和速率不稳定，亟需在吞吐量与稳定性之间取得平衡。

Method: 基于SpaceX Starlink测试床，在六个地理分布的AWS端点进行全球实验评估，对比BBR、Cubic、Vegas和Hybla的性能。提出SLM引导的BBR自适应框架，包含结构化BBR状态编码器、LoRA参数高效微调、以及约束网络头部生成可行 pacing 动作，使用GPT-2、T5、GPT-Neo、SmolLM2四种小语言模型。

Result: BBR在LEO场景下吞吐量始终优于Cubic、Vegas和Hybla，但重传开销显著更高。SLM引导的BBR框架能在保持BBR吞吐优势的同时大幅降低重传率，且轻量级SLM（如SmolLM2）性能与大型语言模型相当，计算成本更低。

Conclusion: 小语言模型可以有效指导LEO卫星互联网场景下的拥塞控制决策，解决BBR的吞吐-稳定性权衡问题，为未来非地面网络中的智能传输层设计提供了可行且低开销的方案。

Abstract: Low Earth Orbit (LEO) satellite Internet introduces rapid path variability, intermittent capacity shifts, and non-terrestrial delay dynamics that challenge transport-layer congestion control. Although Bottleneck Bandwidth and Round-trip propagation time (BBR) achieves high throughput in such environments, its aggressive bandwidth probing can cause excessive retransmissions and unstable pacing over LEO links. This paper presents a global experimental evaluation of BBR over a SpaceX Starlink testbed spanning six geographically distributed AWS endpoints and compares its behaviour against Cubic, Vegas, and Hybla under isolated and competing traffic scenarios. The measurements show that BBR consistently delivers superior throughput but incurs significantly higher retransmission overhead, revealing a critical throughput-stability trade-off in LEO satellite Internet. To address this limitation, we propose a Small Language Model (SLM)-guided BBR adaptation framework that learns phase-safe pacing-gain decisions from real Starlink traces. The framework combines a structured BBR state encoder, LoRA-based parameter-efficient fine-tuning, and a constrained networking head to generate feasible pacing actions with low inference latency. Evaluation using GPT-2, T5, GPT-Neo, and SmolLM2 shows that lightweight SLMs can retain BBR's throughput advantage while substantially reducing retransmissions, with performance comparable to larger language models but at much lower computational cost.

</details>


### [143] [PHaul: A PPO-based forwarding agent for Sub6 enhanced Integrated Access and Backhaul networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07584)
*Jorge Pueyo,Daniel Camps-Mur and,Miguel Catalan-Cid*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出PHaul，一种结合Sub6和毫米波的IAB回传网络转发引擎，通过离线路径选择与在线深度强化学习（PPO）相结合的方式，在10秒内完成流到路径的映射，相比传统启发式方法可提升最高36%的吞吐量效率和20%的公平性，并对拓扑变化具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3GPP IAB网络通过重用频谱实现低成本毫米波接入，但回传链路是性能瓶颈且严重依赖视距（LoS）条件。为缓解LoS依赖并提升回传网络的容量和鲁棒性，作者提出用Sub6链路补充毫米波回传，形成Sub6增强型IAB网络，并需要高效的转发策略来利用可用容量。

Method: 提出了PHaul转发引擎，包含两个核心组件：1）离线路径选择启发式算法；2）基于近端策略优化（PPO）的在线深度强化学习（DRL）智能体。PHaul利用IAB无线回传的网络数字孪生体，定期采样输入流量并更新流到路径的映射，执行时间低于10秒。

Result: 在多种网络配置下，PHaul相比两种对比启发式方法，吞吐量效率提升高达36%，公平性提升高达20%。此外，PHaul对训练与推理阶段之间网络拓扑的差异（如链路故障导致）具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: PHaul作为Sub6增强型IAB网络的转发引擎，能有效提升回传网络的容量和鲁棒性，且在实际部署场景中具备可行性（低延迟、高鲁棒性），为未来IAB网络的优化提供了新思路。

Abstract: 3GPP Integrated Access and Backhaul (IAB) allows operators to deploy outdoor mm-wave access networks in a cost-efficient manner, by reusing the same spectrum in access and backhaul. In IAB networks the performance bottleneck is the wireless backhaul segment, where efficient forwarding strategies are needed to effectively use the available capacity. In addition, the performance of the mm-wave IAB backhaul segment is contingent on the availability of line of sight (LoS) conditions in the selected deployment sites. To mitigate LoS dependence, in this paper, we propose to complement the mm-wave backhaul segment of IAB networks with additional Sub6 backhaul links, which contribute to the capacity and robustness of the backhaul network. We refer to IAB networks combining Sub6 and mm-wave links in the backhaul as Sub6 enhanced IAB networks. In this context, the main contribution of this paper is PHaul, a forwarding engine for Sub6 enhanced IAB networks that accomodates different traffic engineering criteria, and combines an offline path selection heuristic with an online Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) agent based on Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO). By leveraging a network digital twin of the IAB wireless backhaul, PHaul periodically samples the input traffic of the backhaul network and updates flow to path mappings, with execution times below 10 seconds in realistic backhaul topologies. We present an exhaustive performance evaluation, where we demonstrate that PHaul can achieve gains of up to 36\% in throughput efficiency and of up to 20\% in fairness, when compared against two alternative heuristics in a wide range of network configurations. We also demonstrate that PHaul is robust to differences between the network topologies considered in the training and inference phases, which can occur in practice due to link failures.

</details>
